# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                  | HTTP Method | Function Name          | Rendered Template               | Context Variables (Name: Type)                                                     |
|---------------------------|-------------|------------------------|--------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /** (root)                | GET         | root_redirect          | redirect to dashboard           | None                                                                              |
| /dashboard                | GET         | dashboard              | dashboard.html                 | devices_summary: dict (total: int, active: int, offline: int)
  rooms_summary: list of dict {room_name: str, device_count: int}            |
| /devices                  | GET         | device_list            | device_list.html               | devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, device_type: str, room: str, status: str}                      |
| /device/<int:device_id>   | GET         | device_control         | device_control.html            | device: dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, status: str, power: str, brightness: (int or None), temperature: (int or None), mode: str} |
| /device/<int:device_id>/control | POST        | device_control_post    | redirect to /device/<device_id> or error page | updated device data from form (handled internally)                             |
| /add_device               | GET         | add_device             | add_device.html                | rooms: list of str (room names)
  device_types: list of str (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)                      |
| /add_device               | POST        | add_device_post        | redirect to /devices or error page | new device data from form (handled internally)                                |
| /automation               | GET         | automation_rules       | automation.html                | rules: list of dict {rule_id: int, rule_name: str, trigger_type: str, trigger_value: str, action_device_id: int, action_type: str, enabled: bool}
  devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str}                      |
| /automation               | POST        | add_automation_rule    | redirect to /automation or error page | new automation rule data from form (handled internally)                      |
| /energy                   | GET         | energy_report          | energy_report.html             | energy_summary: dict (total_kwh: float, estimated_cost: float)
  energy_logs: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, date: str, consumption_kwh: float}
  filter_date: str or None                                                   |
| /energy/filter            | POST        | energy_filter_post     | redirect to /energy or error page | filter_date: str (parsed from form)                                          |
| /activity                 | GET         | activity_logs          | activity_logs.html             | activities: list of dict {timestamp: str, device_id: int, device_name: str, action: str, details: str}
  search_text: str or None                                                    |
| /activity/search          | POST        | activity_search_post   | redirect to /activity or error page | search_text: str (from form)                                                  |

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Smart Home Dashboard
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page: Div - Main container for dashboard page
  - device-summary: Div - Summary display (total devices, active, offline counts)
  - device-list-button: Button - Navigate to Device List (url_for('device_list'))
  - add-device-button: Button - Navigate to Add Device (url_for('add_device'))
  - automation-button: Button - Navigate to Automation Rules (url_for('automation_rules'))
  - energy-button: Button - Navigate to Energy Report (url_for('energy_report'))
  - activity-button: Button - Navigate to Activity Logs (url_for('activity_logs'))
  - room-list: Div - List of rooms with device counts

### 2. templates/device_list.html
- Page Title: My Devices
- Element IDs:
  - device-list-page: Div - Main container
  - device-table: Table - Showing all devices with columns name, type, room, status, actions
  - control-device-button-{device_id}: Button - Navigate to Device Control (url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 3. templates/add_device.html
- Page Title: Add New Device
- Element IDs:
  - add-device-page: Div - Main container
  - device-name: Input - Text input for device name
  - device-type: Dropdown - Select device type ['Light', 'Thermostat', 'Camera', 'Lock', 'Sensor', 'Appliance']
  - device-room: Dropdown - Select room ['Living Room', 'Bedroom', 'Kitchen', 'Bathroom', 'Garage']
  - submit-device-button: Button - Submits form
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 4. templates/device_control.html
- Page Title: Device Control
- Element IDs:
  - device-control-page: Div - Main container
  - device-name-display: H2 - Displays device name
  - device-status-display: Div - Displays device status (Online/Offline)
  - power-toggle: Button - Toggle device power on/off
  - save-settings-button: Button - Save current settings
  - back-to-devices: Button - Navigate back to Device List (url_for('device_list'))

### 5. templates/automation.html
- Page Title: Automation Rules
- Element IDs:
  - automation-page: Div - Main container
  - rules-table: Table - List all automation rules (name, trigger, action, status)
  - rule-name: Input - Input for rule name
  - trigger-type: Dropdown - Trigger type ['Time', 'Motion', 'Temperature']
  - trigger-value: Input - Text input for trigger value
  - action-device: Dropdown - Select device for action
  - action-type: Dropdown - Action type ['Turn On', 'Turn Off', 'Set Brightness', 'Set Temperature']
  - add-rule-button: Button - Add automation rule
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 6. templates/energy_report.html
- Page Title: Energy Report
- Element IDs:
  - energy-page: Div - Main container
  - energy-summary: Div - Summary of total energy and estimated cost
  - energy-table: Table - Energy consumption details per device with date and kWh
  - date-filter: Input (date) - Filter energy data by date
  - apply-filter-button: Button - Apply date filter
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 7. templates/activity_logs.html
- Page Title: Activity Logs
- Element IDs:
  - activity-page: Div - Main container
  - activity-table: Table - Activity logs with timestamp, device, action, details
  - search-activity: Input - Search activity logs
  - apply-search-button: Button - Apply search
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. data/users.txt
- Filename and Path: data/users.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. email: string (email format)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|john@example.com
  - jane_smith|jane@example.com
- Strict parsing: No header; fields separated by pipe character; exactly 2 fields per line.

### 2. data/devices.txt
- Filename and Path: data/devices.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. device_id: int
  3. device_name: string
  4. device_type: string (one of Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)
  5. room: string (e.g., Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen...)
  6. brand: string
  7. model: string
  8. status: string (Online, Offline)
  9. power: string (on/off)
  10. brightness: int or empty if not applicable
  11. temperature: int or empty if not applicable
  12. mode: string (Auto, Manual or empty)
  13. schedule_time: string (HH:MM format or empty)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  - john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  - jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
- Parsing notes: No header; pipe delimiter; empty fields allowed for non-applicable columns.

### 3. data/rooms.txt
- Filename and Path: data/rooms.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. room_id: int
  3. room_name: string
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Living Room
  - john_doe|2|Bedroom
  - john_doe|3|Kitchen
  - jane_smith|1|Living Room
- Strict parsing: No header; exactly 3 fields per line; pipe-delimited.

### 4. data/automation_rules.txt
- Filename and Path: data/automation_rules.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. rule_id: int
  3. rule_name: string
  4. trigger_type: string (Time, Motion, Temperature)
  5. trigger_value: string (e.g., time '07:00' or motion 'detected', temperature threshold)
  6. action_device_id: int
  7. action_type: string (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature)
  8. action_value: string (can be empty for actions without value)
  9. enabled: bool (true/false in string form)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  - john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  - jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
- Parsing notes: No header; pipe-separated; fields strict.

### 5. data/energy_logs.txt
- Filename and Path: data/energy_logs.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. device_id: int
  3. date: string (YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. consumption_kwh: float
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  - john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  - john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  - jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
- Strict parsing: no header; pipe delimiter; exact fields

### 6. data/activity_logs.txt
- Filename and Path: data/activity_logs.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. timestamp: string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS format)
  3. device_id: int
  4. action: string
  5. details: string
- Examples:
  - john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  - john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  - jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
- Parsing notes: no header; pipe-delimited; exact 5 fields per line

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>Activity Logs</title>
</head>
<body>
    <div id="activity-page">
        <h1>Activity Logs</h1>
        <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('activity_search_post') }}">
            <input type="text" id="search-activity" name="search_text" value="{{ search_text if search_text else '' }}" placeholder="Search activities">
            <button type="submit" id="apply-search-button">Apply Search</button>
        </form>
        <table id="activity-table" border="1">
            <thead>
                <tr>
                    <th>Timestamp</th>
                    <th>Device</th>
                    <th>Action</th>
                    <th>Details</th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                {% for activity in activities %}
                <tr>
                    <td>{{ activity.timestamp }}</td>
                    <td>{{ activity.device_name }}</td>
                    <td>{{ activity.action }}</td>
                    <td>{{ activity.details }}</td>
                </tr>
                {% endfor %}
            </tbody>
        </table>
        <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
    </div>
</body>
</html>

            <input type="number" id="temperature" name="temperature" min="30" max="100" value="{{ device.temperature }}">
            <br>
            {% endif %}
            <label for="mode">Mode:</label>
            <input type="text" id="mode" name="mode" value="{{ device.mode }}">

            <button type="submit" id="save-settings-button">Save Settings</button>
        </form>
        <button id="back-to-devices" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('device_list') }}'">Back to Devices</button>

data/users.txt - Filename and Path: data/users.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. email: string (email format) - Examples:   - john_doe|john@example.com   - jane_smith|jane@example.com - Strict parsing: No header; fields separated by pipe character; exactly 2 fields per line.  ### 2. data/devices.txt - Filename and Path: data/devices.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. device_id: int   3. device_name: string   4. device_type: string (one of Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)   5. room: string (e.g., Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen...)   6. brand: string   7. model: string   8. status: string (Online, Offline)   9. power: string (on/off)   10. brightness: int or empty if not applicable   11. temperature: int or empty if not applicable   12. mode: string (Auto, Manual or empty)   13. schedule_time: string (HH:MM format or empty) - Examples:   - john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|   - john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00   - jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual| - Parsing notes: No header; pipe delimiter; empty fields allowed for non-applicable columns.  ### 3. data/rooms.txt - Filename and Path: data/rooms.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. room_id: int   3. room_name: string - Examples:   - john_doe|1|Living Room   - john_doe|2|Bedroom   - john_doe|3|Kitchen   - jane_smith|1|Living Room - Strict parsing: No header; exactly 3 fields per line; pipe-delimited.  ### 4. data/automation_rules.txt - Filename and Path: data/automation_rules.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. rule_id: int   3. rule_name: string   4. trigger_type: string (Time, Motion, Temperature)   5. trigger_value: string (e.g., time '07:00' or motion 'detected', temperature threshold)   6. action_device_id: int   7. action_type: string (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature)   8. action_value: string (can be empty for actions without value)   9. enabled: bool (true/false in string form) - Examples:   - john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true   - john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true   - jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true - Parsing notes: No header; pipe-separated; fields strict.  ### 5. data/energy_logs.txt - Filename and Path: data/energy_logs.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. device_id: int   3. date: string (YYYY-MM-DD format)   4. consumption_kwh: float - Examples:   - john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5   - john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3   - john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6   - jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2 - Strict parsing: no header; pipe delimiter; exact fields  ### 6. data/activity_logs.txt - Filename and Path: data/activity_logs.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. timestamp: string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS format)   3. device_id: int   4. action: string   5. details: string - Examples:   - john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights   - john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72   - jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control - Parsing notes: no header; pipe-delimited; exact 5 fields per line  ---
  [app.py] from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request import os from datetime import datetime  app = Flask(__name__) app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'  # Paths to data files USERS_FILE = 'data/users.txt' DEVICES_FILE = 'data/devices.txt' AUTOMATION_FILE = 'data/automation_rules.txt' ENERGY_LOGS_FILE = 'data/energy_logs.txt' ACTIVITY_LOGS_FILE = 'data/activity_logs.txt'  # Helper functions  def read_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields_count=None):     """Read a pipe-delimited file and return a list of lists of fields"""     entries = []     if not os.path.exists(filename):         return entries     with open(filename, 'r') as f:         for line in f:             line = line.strip()             if not line:                 continue             parts = line.split('|')             if fields_count and len(parts) != fields_count:                 continue             entries.append(parts)     return entries  # Routes  @app.route('/') def root():     return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))  @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard():     # Read devices and create summary     devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)     # devices_data format: username|device_id|room|device_name|device_type|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode     rooms_summary = {}     devices_list = []     if devices_data:         for d in devices_data:             if len(d) < 10:                 continue             username, device_id, room, device_name, device_type, status, power, brightness, temperature, mode = d             if room not in rooms_summary:                 rooms_summary[room] = 0             rooms_summary[room] += 1             devices_list.append({                 'device_id': int(device_id),                 'device_name': device_name,                 'device_type': device_type,                 'room': room,                 'status': status             })     devices_summary = {         'total': len(devices_list),         'rooms': [{'room_name': rn, 'device_count': cnt} for rn, cnt in rooms_summary.items()]     }     return render_template('dashboard.html', devices_summary=devices_summary, devices_list=devices_list)  @app.route('/device/<int:device_id>') def device_control(device_id):     # Find device by id     devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)     device = None     for d in devices_data:         if len(d) < 10:             continue         username, d_id, room, device_name, device_type, status, power, brightness, temperature, mode = d         if int(d_id) == device_id:             device = {                 'device_id': int(d_id),                 'device_name': device_name,                 'status': status,                 'power': power,                 'brightness': int(brightness) if brightness.isdigit() else None if brightness == '' else None,                 'temperature': int(temperature) if temperature.isdigit() else None if temperature == '' else None,                 'mode': mode             }             break     if not device:         return "Device not found", 404     return render_template('device_control.html', device=device)  @app.route('/add_device', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def add_device():     if request.method == 'GET':         # Gather rooms and device types from existing data         devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)         rooms = set()         device_types = set(['Light', 'Thermostat', 'Camera', 'Lock', 'Sensor', 'Appliance'])         for d in devices_data:             if len(d) < 10:                 continue             rooms.add(d[2])  # room         return render_template('add_device.html', rooms=sorted(rooms), device_types=sorted(device_types))     else:         # POST: add device to the file         device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()         device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()         device_room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()         # Simplified device_id generation: max existing id + 1         devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)         max_id = 0         for d in devices_data:             if len(d) < 10:                 continue             try:                 did = int(d[1])                 if did > max_id:                     max_id = did             except ValueError:                 continue         new_device_id = max_id + 1         # Default new device values         new_device_line = f"default_user|{new_device_id}|{device_room}|{device_name}|{device_type}|Offline|off|||Auto|"         with open(DEVICES_FILE, 'a') as f:             f.write(new_device_line + '\n')         return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))  @app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def automation():     if request.method == 'GET':         # Read automation rules and devices         rules_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(AUTOMATION_FILE, fields_count=7)         rules = []         for r in rules_data:             try:                 rules.append({                     'rule_id': int(r[0]),                     'rule_name': r[1],                     'trigger_type': r[2],                     'trigger_value': r[3],                     'action_device_id': int(r[4]),                     'action_type': r[5],                     'enabled': r[6].lower() == 'true'                 })             except Exception:                 continue         devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)         devices = []         for d in devices_data:             if len(d) < 10:                 continue             try:                 devices.append({'device_id': int(d[1]), 'device_name': d[3]})             except Exception:                 continue         return render_template('automation.html', rules=rules, devices=devices)     else:         # POST: Add new rule         rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name','').strip()         trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type','').strip()         trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value','').strip()         action_device_id = request.form.get('action_device_id','').strip()         action_type = request.form.get('action_type','').strip()         enabled        rules_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(AUTOMATION_FILE, fields_count=7)         max_id = 0         for r in rules_data:             try:                 rid = int(r[0])                 if rid > max_id:                     max_id = rid             except:                 continue         new_rule_id = max_id + 1          new_rule_line = f"{new_rule_id}|{rule_name}|{trigger_type}|{trigger_value}|{action_device_id_int}|{action_type}|{str(enabled).lower()}"         with open(AUTOMATION_FILE, 'a') as f:             f.write(new_rule_line + '\n')          return redirect(url_for('automation'))  @app.route('/energy_report', methods=['GET']) def energy_report():     # Read energy logs     energy_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, fields_count=4)     energy_logs = []     total_kwh = 0.0     for e in energy_data:         try:             energy_logs.append({                 'device_id': int(e[1]),                 'device_name': e[0],                 'date': e[2],                 'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])             })             total_kwh += float(e[3])         except Exception:             continue     energy_summary = {'total_kwh': total_kwh}     return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=energy_logs, filter_date=None)  @app.route('/energy_filter', methods=['POST']) def energy_filter_post():     filter_date_str = request.form.get('filter_date','')     try:         filter_date_obj = datetime.strptime(filter_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')     except Exception:         return render_template('error.html', message="Invalid date format")     energy_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, fields_count=4)     filtered_logs = []     filtered_kwh = 0.0     for e in energy_data:         if len(e) < 4:             continue         try:             if e[2] == filter_date_str:                 filtered_logs.append({                     'device_id': int(e[1]),                     'device_name': e[0],                     'date': e[2],                     'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])                 })                 filtered_kwh += float(e[3])         except:             continue     energy_summary = {'total_kwh': filtered_kwh}     return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=filtered_logs, filter_date=filter_date_str)  @app.route('/activity_logs', methods=['GET']) def activity_logs():     search_text = request.args.get('search_text','').strip()     activity_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(ACTIVITY_LOGS_FILE, fields_count=5)     activities = []     for a in activity_data:         if len(a) < 5:             continue         timestamp, device_id, action, details = a[1], a[2], a[3], a[4]         device_name = ''         # Find device name         devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)         for d in devices_data:             if len(d) >= 4 and d[1] == device_id:                 device_name = d[3]                 break         if search_text and search_text.lower() not in device_id.isdigit() else device_id,             'device_name': device_name,             'action': action,             'details': details         })     return render_template('activity_logs.html', # SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                  | HTTP Method | Function Name          | Rendered Template               | Context Variables (Name: Type)                                                     |
|---------------------------|-------------|------------------------|--------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /** (root)                | GET         | root_redirect          | redirect to dashboard           | None                                                                              |
| /dashboard                | GET         | dashboard              | dashboard.html                 | devices_summary: dict (total: int, active: int, offline: int)
  rooms_summary: list of dict {room_name: str, device_count: int}            |
| /devices                  | GET         | device_list            | device_list.html               | devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, device_type: str, room: str, status: str}                      |
| /device/<int:device_id>   | GET         | device_control         | device_control.html            | device: dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, status: str, power: str, brightness: (int or None), temperature: (int or None), mode: str} |
| /device/<int:device_id>/control | POST        | device_control_post    | redirect to /device/<device_id> or error page | updated device data from form (handled internally)                             |
| /add_device               | GET         | add_device             | add_device.html                | rooms: list of str (room names)
  device_types: list of str (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)                      |
| /add_device               | POST        | add_device_post        | redirect to /devices or error page | new device data from form (handled internally)                                |
| /automation               | GET         | automation_rules       | automation.html                | rules: list of dict {rule_id: int, rule_name: str, trigger_type: str, trigger_value: str, action_device_id: int, action_type: str, enabled: bool}
  devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str}                      |
| /automation               | POST        | add_automation_rule    | redirect to /automation or error page | new automation rule data from form (handled internally)                      |
| /energy                   | GET         | energy_report          | energy_report.html             | energy_summary: dict (total_kwh: float, estimated_cost: float)
  energy_logs: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, date: str, consumption_kwh: float}
  filter_date: str or None                                                   |
| /energy/filter            | POST        | energy_filter_post     | redirect to /energy or error page | filter_date: str (parsed from form)                                          |
| /activity                 | GET         | activity_logs          | activity_logs.html             | activities: list of dict {timestamp: str, device_id: int, device_name: str, action: str, details: str}
  search_text: str or None                                                    |
| /activity/search          | POST        | activity_search_post   | redirect to /activity or error page | search_text: str (from form)                                                  |

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. data/users.txt
- Filename and Path: data/users.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. email: string (email format)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|john@example.com
  - jane_smith|jane@example.com
- Strict parsing: No header; fields separated by pipe character; exactly 2 fields per line.

### 2. data/devices.txt
- Filename and Path: data/devices.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. device_id: int
  3. device_name: string
  4. device_type: string (one of Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)
  5. room: string (e.g., Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen...)
  6. brand: string
  7. model: string
  8. status: string (Online, Offline)
  9. power: string (on/off)
  10. brightness: int or empty if not applicable
  11. temperature: int or empty if not applicable
  12. mode: string (Auto, Manual or empty)
  13. schedule_time: string (HH:MM format or empty)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  - john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  - jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
- Parsing notes: No header; pipe delimiter; empty fields allowed for non-applicable columns.

### 3. data/rooms.txt
- Filename and Path: data/rooms.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. room_id: int
  3. room_name: string
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Living Room
  - john_doe|2|Bedroom
  - john_doe|3|Kitchen
  - jane_smith|1|Living Room
- Strict parsing: No header; exactly 3 fields per line; pipe-delimited.

### 4. data/automation_rules.txt
- Filename and Path: data/automation_rules.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. rule_id: int
  3. rule_name: string
  4. trigger_type: string (Time, Motion, Temperature)
  5. trigger_value: string (e.g., time '07:00' or motion 'detected', temperature threshold)
  6. action_device_id: int
  7. action_type: string (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature)
  8. action_value: string (can be empty for actions without value)
  9. enabled: bool (true/false in string form)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  - john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  - jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
- Parsing notes: No header; pipe-separated; fields strict.

### 5. data/energy_logs.txt
- Filename and Path: data/energy_logs.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. device_id: int
  3. date: string (YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. consumption_kwh: float
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  - john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  - john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  - jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
- Strict parsing: no header; pipe delimiter; exact fields

### 6. data/activity_logs.txt
- Filename and Path: data/activity_logs.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. timestamp: string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS format)
  3. device_id: int
  4. action: string
  5. details: string
- Examples:
  - john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  - john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  - jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
- Parsing notes: no header; pipe-delimited; exact 5 fields per line

=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'

# Paths to data files
USERS_FILE = 'data/users.txt'
DEVICES_FILE = 'data/devices.txt'
AUTOMATION_FILE = 'data/automation_rules.txt'
ENERGY_LOGS_FILE = 'data/energy_logs.txt'
ACTIVITY_LOGS_FILE = 'data/activity_logs.txt'

# Helper functions

def read_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields_count=None):
    """Read a pipe-delimited file and return a list of lists of fields"""
    entries = []
    if not os.path.exists(filename):
        return entries
    with open(filename, 'r') as f:
        for line in f:
            line = line.strip()
            if not line:
                continue
            parts = line.split('|')
            if fields_count and len(parts) != fields_count:
                continue
            entries.append(parts)
    return entries

# Routes

@app.route('/')
def root():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    # Read devices and create summary
    devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)
    # devices_data format: username|device_id|room|device_name|device_type|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode
    rooms_summary = {}
    devices_list = []
    if devices_data:
        for d in devices_data:
            if len(d) < 10:
                continue
            username, device_id, room, device_name, device_type, status, power, brightness, temperature, mode = d
            if room not in rooms_summary:
                rooms_summary[room] = 0
            rooms_summary[room] += 1
            devices_list.append({
                'device_id': int(device_id),
                'device_name': device_name,
                'device_type': device_type,
                'room': room,
                'status': status
            })
    devices_summary = {
        'total': len(devices_list),
        'rooms': [{'room_name': rn, 'device_count': cnt} for rn, cnt in rooms_summary.items()]
    }
    return render_template('dashboard.html', devices_summary=devices_summary, devices_list=devices_list)

@app.route('/device/<int:device_id>')
def device_control(device_id):
    # Find device by id
    devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)
    device = None
    for d in devices_data:
        if len(d) < 10:
            continue
        username, d_id, room, device_name, device_type, status, power, brightness, temperature, mode = d
        if int(d_id) == device_id:
            device = {
                'device_id': int(d_id),
                'device_name': device_name,
                'status': status,
                'power': power,
                'brightness': int(brightness) if brightness.isdigit() else None if brightness == '' else None,
                'temperature': int(temperature) if temperature.isdigit() else None if temperature == '' else None,
                'mode': mode
            }
            break
    if not device:
        return "Device not found", 404
    return render_template('device_control.html', device=device)

@app.route('/add_device', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def add_device():
    if request.method == 'GET':
        # Gather rooms and device types from existing data
        devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)
        rooms = set()
        device_types = set(['Light', 'Thermostat', 'Camera', 'Lock', 'Sensor', 'Appliance'])
        for d in devices_data:
            if len(d) < 10:
                continue
            rooms.add(d[2])  # room
        return render_template('add_device.html', rooms=sorted(rooms), device_types=sorted(device_types))
    else:
        # POST: add device to the file
        device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()
        device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
        device_room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()
        # Simplified device_id generation: max existing id + 1
        devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)
        max_id = 0
        for d in devices_data:
            if len(d) < 10:
                continue
            try:
                did = int(d[1])
                if did > max_id:
                    max_id = did
            except ValueError:
                continue
        new_device_id = max_id + 1
        # Default new device values
        new_device_line = f"default_user|{new_device_id}|{device_room}|{device_name}|{device_type}|Offline|off|||Auto|"
        with open(DEVICES_FILE, 'a') as f:
            f.write(new_device_line + '\n')
        return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

@app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def automation():
    if request.method == 'GET':
        # Read automation rules and devices
        rules_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(AUTOMATION_FILE, fields_count=7)
        rules = []
        for r in rules_data:
            try:
                rules.append({
                    'rule_id': int(r[0]),
                    'rule_name': r[1],
                    'trigger_type': r[2],
                    'trigger_value': r[3],
                    'action_device_id': int(r[4]),
                    'action_type': r[5],
                    'enabled': r[6].lower() == 'true'
                })
            except Exception:
                continue
        devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)
        devices = []
        for d in devices_data:
            if len(d) < 10:
                continue
            try:
                devices.append({'device_id': int(d[1]), 'device_name': d[3]})
            except Exception:
                continue
        return render_template('automation.html', rules=rules, devices=devices)
    else:
        # POST: Add new rule
        rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name','').strip()
        trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type','').strip()
        trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value','').strip()
        action_device_id = request.form.get('action_device_id','').strip()
        action_type = request.form.get('action_type','').strip()
        enabled = request.form.get('enabled','off') == 'on'

        try:
            action_device_id_int = int(action_device_id)
        except:
            action_device_id_int = 0

        # Generate new rule_id
        rules_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(AUTOMATION_FILE, fields_count=7)
        max_id = 0
        for r in rules_data:
            try:
                rid = int(r[0])
                if rid > max_id:
                    max_id = rid
            except:
                continue
        new_rule_id = max_id + 1

        new_rule_line = f"{new_rule_id}|{rule_name}|{trigger_type}|{trigger_value}|{action_device_id_int}|{action_type}|{str(enabled).lower()}"
        with open(AUTOMATION_FILE, 'a') as f:
            f.write(new_rule_line + '\n')

        return redirect(url_for('automation'))

@app.route('/energy_report', methods=['GET'])
def energy_report():
    # Read energy logs
    energy_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, fields_count=4)
    energy_logs = []
    total_kwh = 0.0
    for e in energy_data:
        try:
            energy_logs.append({
                'device_id': int(e[1]),
                'device_name': e[0],
                'date': e[2],
                'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])
            })
            total_kwh += float(e[3])
        except Exception:
            continue
    energy_summary = {'total_kwh': total_kwh}
    return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=energy_logs, filter_date=None)

@app.route('/energy_filter', methods=['POST'])
def energy_filter_post():
    filter_date_str = request.form.get('filter_date','')
    try:
        filter_date_obj = datetime.strptime(filter_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
    except Exception:
        return render_template('error.html', message="Invalid date format")
    energy_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, fields_count=4)
    filtered_logs = []
    filtered_kwh = 0.0
    for e in energy_data:
        if len(e) < 4:
            continue
        try:
            if e[2] == filter_date_str:
                filtered_logs.append({
                    'device_id': int(e[1]),
                    'device_name': e[0],
                    'date': e[2],
                    'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])
                })
                filtered_kwh += float(e[3])
        except:
            continue
    energy_summary = {'total_kwh': filtered_kwh}
    return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=filtered_logs, filter_date=filter_date_str)

@app.route('/activity_logs', methods=['GET'])
def activity_logs():
    search_text = request.args.get('search_text','').strip()
    activity_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(ACTIVITY_LOGS_FILE, fields_count=5)
    activities = []
    for a in activity_data:
        if len(a) < 5:
            continue
        timestamp, device_id, action, details = a[1], a[2], a[3], a[4]
        device_name = ''
        # Find device name
        devices_data = read_pipe_delimited_file(DEVICES_FILE)
        for d in devices_data:
            if len(d) >= 4 and d[1] == device_id:
                device_name = d[3]
                break
        if search_text and search_text.lower() not in action.lower() and search_text.lower() not in details.lower():
            continue
        activities.append({
            'timestamp': timestamp,
            'device_id': int(device_id) if device_id.isdigit() else device_id,
            'device_name': device_name,
            'action': action,
            'details': details
        })
    return render_template('activity_logs.html', activities=activities, search_text=search_text)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

data/users.txt - Filename and Path: data/users.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. email: string (email format) - Examples:   - john_doe|john@example.com   - jane_smith|jane@example.com - Strict parsing: No header; fields separated by pipe character; exactly 2 fields per line.  ### 2. data/devices.txt - Filename and Path: data/devices.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. device_id: int   3. device_name: string   4. device_type: string (one of Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)   5. room: string (e.g., Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen...)   6. brand: string   7. model: string   8. status: string (Online, Offline)   9. power: string (on/off)   10. brightness: int or empty if not applicable   11. temperature: int or empty if not applicable   12. mode: string (Auto, Manual or empty)   13. schedule_time: string (HH:MM format or empty) - Examples:   - john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|   - john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00   - jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual| - Parsing notes: No header; pipe delimiter; empty fields allowed for non-applicable columns.  ### 3. data/rooms.txt - Filename and Path: data/rooms.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. room_id: int   3. room_name: string - Examples:   - john_doe|1|Living Room   - john_doe|2|Bedroom   - john_doe|3|Kitchen   - jane_smith|1|Living Room - Strict parsing: No header; exactly 3 fields per line; pipe-delimited.  ### 4. data/automation_rules.txt - Filename and Path: data/automation_rules.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. rule_id: int   3. rule_name: string   4. trigger_type: string (Time, Motion, Temperature)   5. trigger_value: string (e.g., time '07:00' or motion 'detected', temperature threshold)   6. action_device_id: int   7. action_type: string (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature)   8. action_value: string (can be empty for actions without value)   9. enabled: bool (true/false in string form) - Examples:   - john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true   - john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true   - jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true - Parsing notes: No header; pipe-separated; fields strict.  ### 5. data/energy_logs.txt - Filename and Path: data/energy_logs.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. device_id: int   3. date: string (YYYY-MM-DD format)   4. consumption_kwh: float - Examples:   - john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5   - john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3   - john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6   - jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2 - Strict parsing: no header; pipe delimiter; exact fields  ### 6. data/activity_logs.txt - Filename and Path: data/activity_logs.txt - Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):   1. username: string   2. timestamp: string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS format)   3. device_id: int   4. action: string   5. details: string - Examples:   - john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights   - john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72   - jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control - Parsing notes: no header; pipe-delimited; exact 5 fields per line  ---

Util  def read_pipe_file(filename, expected_fields=None):     entries = []     if not os.path.exists(filename):         return entries     with open(filename) as f:         for line in f:             line = line.strip()             if not line:                 continue             parts = line.split('|')             if expected_fields is not None and len(parts) != expected_fields:                 continue             entries.append(parts)     return entries  # Routes  @app.route('/') def root_redirect():     return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))  @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard(): device_type, brand, status(Online/Offline), power(on/off), brightness, temperature, mode, schedule_time         try:             username = d[0]             device_id = int(d[1])             room = d[2]             device_name = d[3]             device_type = d[4]             status = d[6]         except:             continue         rooms[room] = rooms.get(room, 0) + 1         devices_list.append({             'device_id': device_id,             'device_name': device_name,             'device_type': device_type,             'room': room,             'status': status         })     devices_summary = {         'total': len(devices_list),         'rooms': [{'room_name': k, 'device_count': v} for k,v in rooms.items()]     }     return render_template('dashboard.html', devices_summary=devices_summary, rooms_summary=devices_summary['rooms'], devices_list=devices_list)  @app.route('/device_list') def device_list():     devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, # SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                  | HTTP Method | Function Name          | Rendered Template               | Context Variables (Name: Type)                                                     |
|---------------------------|-------------|------------------------|--------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /** (root)                | GET         | root_redirect          | redirect to dashboard           | None                                                                              |
| /dashboard                | GET         | dashboard              | dashboard.html                 | devices_summary: dict (total: int, active: int, offline: int)
  rooms_summary: list of dict {room_name: str, device_count: int}            |
| /devices                  | GET         | device_list            | device_list.html               | devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, device_type: str, room: str, status: str}                      |
| /device/<int:device_id>   | GET         | device_control         | device_control.html            | device: dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, status: str, power: str, brightness: (int or None), temperature: (int or None), mode: str} |
| /device/<int:device_id>/control | POST        | device_control_post    | redirect to /device/<device_id> or error page | updated device data from form (handled internally)                             |
| /add_device               | GET         | add_device             | add_device.html                | rooms: list of str (room names)
  device_types: list of str (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)                      |
| /add_device               | POST        | add_device_post        | redirect to /devices or error page | new device data from form (handled internally)                                |
| /automation               | GET         | automation_rules       | automation.html                | rules: list of dict {rule_id: int, rule_name: str, trigger_type: str, trigger_value: str, action_device_id: int, action_type: str, enabled: bool}
  devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str}                      |
| /automation               | POST        | add_automation_rule    | redirect to /automation or error page | new automation rule data from form (handled internally)                      |
| /energy                   | GET         | energy_report          | energy_report.html             | energy_summary: dict (total_kwh: float, estimated_cost: float)
  energy_logs: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, date: str, consumption_kwh: float}
  filter_date: str or None                                                   |
| /energy/filter            | POST        | energy_filter_post     | redirect to /energy or error page | filter_date: str (parsed from form)                                          |
| /activity                 | GET         | activity_logs          | activity_logs.html             | activities: list of dict {timestamp: str, device_id: int, device_name: str, action: str, details: str}
  search_text: str or None                                                    |
| /activity/search          | POST        | activity_search_post   | redirect to /activity or error page | search_text: str (from form)                                                  |

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Smart Home Dashboard
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page: Div - Main container for dashboard page
  - device-summary: Div - Summary display (total devices, active, offline counts)
  - device-list-button: Button - Navigate to Device List (url_for('device_list'))
  - add-device-button: Button - Navigate to Add Device (url_for('add_device'))
  - automation-button: Button - Navigate to Automation Rules (url_for('automation_rules'))
  - energy-button: Button - Navigate to Energy Report (url_for('energy_report'))
  - activity-button: Button - Navigate to Activity Logs (url_for('activity_logs'))
  - room-list: Div - List of rooms with device counts

### 2. templates/device_list.html
- Page Title: My Devices
- Element IDs:
  - device-list-page: Div - Main container
  - device-table: Table - Showing all devices with columns name, type, room, status, actions
  - control-device-button-{device_id}: Button - Navigate to Device Control (url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 3. templates/add_device.html
- Page Title: Add New Device
- Element IDs:
  - add-device-page: Div - Main container
  - device-name: Input - Text input for device name
  - device-type: Dropdown - Select device type ['Light', 'Thermostat', 'Camera', 'Lock', 'Sensor', 'Appliance']
  - device-room: Dropdown - Select room ['Living Room', 'Bedroom', 'Kitchen', 'Bathroom', 'Garage']
  - submit-device-button: Button - Submits form
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 4. templates/device_control.html
- Page Title: Device Control
- Element IDs:
  - device-control-page: Div - Main container
  - device-name-display: H2 - Displays device name
  - device-status-display: Div - Displays device status (Online/Offline)
  - power-toggle: Button - Toggle device power on/off
  - save-settings-button: Button - Save current settings
  - back-to-devices: Button - Navigate back to Device List (url_for('device_list'))

### 5. templates/automation.html
- Page Title: Automation Rules
- Element IDs:
  - automation-page: Div - Main container
  - rules-table: Table - List all automation rules (name, trigger, action, status)
  - rule-name: Input - Input for rule name
  - trigger-type: Dropdown - Trigger type ['Time', 'Motion', 'Temperature']
  - trigger-value: Input - Text input for trigger value
  - action-device: Dropdown - Select device for action
  - action-type: Dropdown - Action type ['Turn On', 'Turn Off', 'Set Brightness', 'Set Temperature']
  - add-rule-button: Button - Add automation rule
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 6. templates/energy_report.html
- Page Title: Energy Report
- Element IDs:
  - energy-page: Div - Main container
  - energy-summary: Div - Summary of total energy and estimated cost
  - energy-table: Table - Energy consumption details per device with date and kWh
  - date-filter: Input (date) - Filter energy data by date
  - apply-filter-button: Button - Apply date filter
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 7. templates/activity_logs.html
- Page Title: Activity Logs
- Element IDs:
  - activity-page: Div - Main container
  - activity-table: Table - Activity logs with timestamp, device, action, details
  - search-activity: Input - Search activity logs
  - apply-search-button: Button - Apply search
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. data/users.txt
- Filename and Path: data/users.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. email: string (email format)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|john@example.com
  - jane_smith|jane@example.com
- Strict parsing: No header; fields separated by pipe character; exactly 2 fields per line.

### 2. data/devices.txt
- Filename and Path: data/devices.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. device_id: int
  3. device_name: string
  4. device_type: string (one of Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)
  5. room: string (e.g., Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen...)
  6. brand: string
  7. model: string
  8. status: string (Online, Offline)
  9. power: string (on/off)
  10. brightness: int or empty if not applicable
  11. temperature: int or empty if not applicable
  12. mode: string (Auto, Manual or empty)
  13. schedule_time: string (HH:MM format or empty)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  - john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  - jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
- Parsing notes: No header; pipe delimiter; empty fields allowed for non-applicable columns.

### 3. data/rooms.txt
- Filename and Path: data/rooms.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. room_id: int
  3. room_name: string
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Living Room
  - john_doe|2|Bedroom
  - john_doe|3|Kitchen
  - jane_smith|1|Living Room
- Strict parsing: No header; exactly 3 fields per line; pipe-delimited.

### 4. data/automation_rules.txt
- Filename and Path: data/automation_rules.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. rule_id: int
  3. rule_name: string
  4. trigger_type: string (Time, Motion, Temperature)
  5. trigger_value: string (e.g., time '07:00' or motion 'detected', temperature threshold)
  6. action_device_id: int
  7. action_type: string (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature)
  8. action_value: string (can be empty for actions without value)
  9. enabled: bool (true/false in string form)
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  - john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  - jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
- Parsing notes: No header; pipe-separated; fields strict.

### 5. data/energy_logs.txt
- Filename and Path: data/energy_logs.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. device_id: int
  3. date: string (YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. consumption_kwh: float
- Examples:
  - john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  - john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  - john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  - jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
- Strict parsing: no header; pipe delimiter; exact fields

### 6. data/activity_logs.txt
- Filename and Path: data/activity_logs.txt
- Pipe-Delimited Fields (no header):
  1. username: string
  2. timestamp: string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS format)
  3. device_id: int
  4. action: string
  5. details: string
- Examples:
  - john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  - john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  - jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
- Parsing notes: no header; pipe-delimited; exact 5 fields per line

---

=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'

# Data files
USERS_FILE = 'data/users.txt'
DEVICES_FILE = 'data/devices.txt'
AUTOMATION_FILE = 'data/automation_rules.txt'
ENERGY_LOGS_FILE = 'data/energy_logs.txt'
ACTIVITY_LOGS_FILE = 'data/activity_logs.txt'

# Util

def read_pipe_file(filename, expected_fields=None):
    entries = []
    if not os.path.exists(filename):
        return entries
    with open(filename) as f:
        for line in f:
            line = line.strip()
            if not line:
                continue
            parts = line.split('|')
            if expected_fields is not None and len(parts) != expected_fields:
                continue
            entries.append(parts)
    return entries

# Routes

@app.route('/')
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)
    rooms = {}
    devices_list = []
    for d in devices:
        # device fields: username, device_id, device_location (room), device_name, device_type, brand, status(Online/Offline), power(on/off), brightness, temperature, mode, schedule_time
        try:
            username = d[0]
            device_id = int(d[1])
            room = d[2]
            device_name = d[3]
            device_type = d[4]
            status = d[6]
        except:
            continue
        rooms[room] = rooms.get(room, 0) + 1
        devices_list.append({
            'device_id': device_id,
            'device_name': device_name,
            'device_type': device_type,
            'room': room,
            'status': status
        })
    devices_summary = {
        'total': len(devices_list),
        'rooms': [{'room_name': k, 'device_count': v} for k,v in rooms.items()]
    }
    return render_template('dashboard.html', devices_summary=devices_summary, rooms_summary=devices_summary['rooms'], devices_list=devices_list)

@app.route('/device_list')
def device_list():
    devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)
    device_list_data = []
    for d in devices:
        try:
            device_list_data.append({
                'device_id': int(d[1]),
                'device_name': d[3],
                'device_type': d[4],
                'room': d[2],
                'status': d[6]
            })
        except Exception:
            continue
    return render_template('device_list.html', device_list=device_list_data)

@app.route('/device/<int:device_id>')
def device_control(device_id):
    devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)
    device = None
    for d in devices:
        try:
            did = int(d[1])
            if did == device_id:
                brightness = d[8]
                temperature = d[9]
                device = {
                    'device_id': did,
                    'device_name': d[3],
                    'status': d[6],
                    'power': d[7],
                    'brightness': int(brightness) if brightness.isdigit() else None if brightness=='' else None,
                    'temperature': int(temperature) if temperature.isdigit() else None if temperature=='' else None,
                    'mode': d[10]
                }
                break
        except Exception:
            continue
    if device is None:
        return "Device not found", 404
    return render_template('device_control.html', device=device)

@app.route('/add_device', methods=['GET'])
def add_device():
    devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)
    rooms = set()
    for d in devices:
        if len(d) < 13:
            continue
        rooms.add(d[2])
    device_types = ['Light', 'Thermostat', 'Camera', 'Lock', 'Sensor', 'Appliance']
    return render_template('add_device.html', rooms=sorted(rooms), device_types=device_types)

@app.route('/add_device', methods=['POST'])
def add_device_post():
    device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()
    device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
    device_room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()

    devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)
    max_id = 0
    for d in devices:
        try:
            did = int(d[1])
            if did > max_id:
                max_id = did
        except:
            continue
    new_id = max_id + 1

    # Compose new device line - as per data definition (13 fields)
    # username, device_id, room, device_name, device_type, brand (empty), status 'Offline', power 'off', brightness empty, temperature empty, mode 'Auto', schedule_time empty
    new_line = f'default_user|{new_id}|{device_room}|{device_name}|{device_type}|||Offline|off|||Auto|'

    with open(DEVICES_FILE, 'a') as f:
        f.write(new_line + '\n')

    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

@app.route('/automation', methods=['GET'])
def automation():
    rules = []
    rules_data = read_pipe_file(AUTOMATION_FILE, expected_fields=7)
    for r in rules_data:
        try:
            rules.append({
                'rule_id': int(r[0]),
                'rule_name': r[1],
                'trigger_type': r[2],
                'trigger_value': r[3],
                'action_device_id': int(r[4]),
                'action_type': r[5],
                'enabled': r[6].lower() == 'true'
            })
        except:
            continue
    devices = []
    devices_data = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)
    for d in devices_data:
        try:
            devices.append({'device_id': int(d[1]), 'device_name': d[3]})
        except:
            continue
    return render_template('automation.html', rules=rules, devices=devices)

@app.route('/automation', methods=['POST'])
def add_automation_rule():
    rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()
    trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()
    trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()
    action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device_id', '').strip()
    action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()
    enabled = request.form.get('enabled', '') == 'on'

    try:
        action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)
    except:
        action_device_id = 0

    rules_data = read_pipe_file(AUTOMATION_FILE, expected_fields=7)
    max_id = 0
    for r in rules_data:
        try:
            rid = int(r[0])
            if rid > max_id:
                max_id = rid
        except:
            continue
    new_id = max_id + 1
    new_line = f'{new_id}|{rule_name}|{trigger_type}|{trigger_value}|{action_device_id}|{action_type}|{str(enabled).lower()}'

    with open(AUTOMATION_FILE, 'a') as f:
        f.write(new_line + '\n')

    return redirect(url_for('automation'))

@app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])
def energy_report():
    energy_logs = []
    total_kwh = 0.0
    energy_data = read_pipe_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, expected_fields=4)
    for e in energy_data:
        try:
            energy_logs.append({
                'device_id': int(e[1]),
                'device_name': e[0],
                'date': e[2],
                'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])
            })
            total_kwh += float(e[3])
        except:
            continue
    energy_summary = {'total_kwh': total_kwh, 'estimated_cost': total_kwh * 0.12} # Assume cost per kWh
    return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=energy_logs, filter_date=None)

@app.route('/energy/filter', methods=['POST'])
def energy_filter_post():
    filter_date = request.form.get('filter_date', '').strip()
    try:
        datetime.strptime(filter_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
    except:
        return render_template('error.html', message='Invalid date format')
    energy_logs = []
    total_kwh = 0.0
    energy_data = read_pipe_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, expected_fields=4)
    for e in energy_data:
        if e[2] == filter_date:
            try:
                energy_logs.append({
                    'device_id': int(e[1]),
                    'device_name': e[0],
                    'date': e[2],
                    'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])
                })
                total_kwh += float(e[3])
            except:
                continue
    energy_summary = {'total_kwh': total_kwh, 'estimated_cost': total_kwh * 0.12}
    return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=energy_logs, filter_date=filter_date)

@app.route('/activity', methods=['GET'])
def activity_logs():
    search_text = request.args.get('search_text', '').strip().lower()
    activities = []
    activity_data = read_pipe_file(ACTIVITY_LOGS_FILE, expected_fields=5)
    devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)

    # Index devices by device_id for fast lookup
    device_map = {}
    for d in devices:
        try:
            device_map[int(d[1])] = d[3]
        except:
            continue

    for entry in activity_data:
        try:
            timestamp = entry[1]
            device_id = int(entry[2])
            action = entry[3]
            details = entry[4]
            device_name = device_map.get(device_id, '')
            if search_text and search_text not in action.lower() and search_text not in details.lower():
                continue
            activities.append({
                'timestamp': timestamp,
                'device_id': device_id,
                'device_name': device_name,
                'action': action,
                'details': details
            })
        except:
            continue
    return render_template('activity_logs.html', activities=activities, search_text=search_text)

@app.route('/activity', methods=['POST'])
def activity_search_post():
    search_text = request.form.get('search_text', '')
    return redirect(url_for('activity_logs', search_text=search_text))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

Utility to read pipe-delimited files  def read_pipe_file(filename, expected_fields=None):     entries = []     if not os.path.exists(filename):         return entries     with open(filename) as file:         for line in file:             line=line.strip()             if not line:                 continue             parts = line.split('|')             if expected_fields and len(parts) != expected_fields:                 continue             entries.append(parts)     return entries  # Route: root redirects to dashboard @app.route('/') def root_redirect():     return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))  # Route: dashboard page @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard():     devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)     rooms = {}     devices_list = []     for d in devices:         try:             # username, device_id, room, device_name, device_type, brand, status, power, brightness, temperature, mode, schedule_time             device_id = int(d[1])             room = d[2]             device_name = d[3]             device_type = d[4]             status = d[6]         except:             continue         rooms[room] = rooms.get(room, 0) + 1         devices_list.append({             'device_id': device_id,             'device_name': device_name,             'device_type': device_type,             'room': room,             'status': status         })     devices_summary = {         'total': len(devices_list),         'rooms': [{'room_name': r, 'device_count': c} for r, c in rooms.items()]     }     return render_template('dashboard.html', devices_summary=devices_summary, rooms_summary=devices_summary['rooms'], devices_list=devices_list)  # Route: device control POST (to update device) @app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['POST']) def device_control_post(device_id):     devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)     new_devices = []     for d in devices:         try:             did = int(d[1])             if did == device_id:                 # Route: add_device POST @app.route('/add_device', methods=['POST']) def add_device_post():     device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()     device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()     device_room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()      devices = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)     max_id = 0     for d in devices:         try:             did = int(d[1])             if did > max_id:                 max_id = did         except:             continue     new_id = max_id + 1      # Route: automation GET @app.route('/automation', methods=['GET']) def automation():     rules = []     rules_raw = read_pipe_file(AUTOMATION_FILE, expected_fields=7)     for r in rules_raw:         try:             rules.append({                 'rule_id': int(r[0]),                 'rule_name': r[1],                 'trigger_type': r[2],                 'trigger_value': r[3],                 'action_device_id': int(r[4]),                 'action_type': r[5],                 'enabled': r[6].lower() == 'true'             })         except:             continue     devices_raw = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)     devices = []     for d in devices_raw:         try:             devices.append({'device_id': int(d[1]), 'device_name': d[3]})         except:             continue     return render_template('automation.html', rules=rules, devices=devices)  # Route: energy report GET @app.route('/energy', methods=['GET']) def energy_report():     energy_logs = []     total_kwh = 0.0     energy_raw = read_pipe_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, expected_fields=4)     for e in energy_raw:         try:             energy_logs.append({                 'device_id': int(e[1]),                 'device_name': e[0],                 'date': e[2],                 'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])             })             total_kwh += float(e[3])         except:             continue     energy_summary = {'total_kwh': total_kwh, 'estimated_cost': total_kwh * 0.12}     return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=energy_logs, filter_date=None)  # Route: energy filter POST @app.route('/energy/filter', methods=['POST']) def energy_filter_post():     filter_date = request.form.get('filter_date', '').strip()     try:         datetime.strptime(filter_date, '%Y-%m-%d')     except:         return render_template('error.html', message='Invalid date format')     energy_logs = []     total_kwh = 0.0     energy_raw = read_pipe_file(ENERGY_LOGS_FILE, expected_fields=4)     for e in energy_raw:         if e[2] == filter_date:             try:                 energy_logs.append({                     'device_id': int(e[1]),                     'device_name': e[0],                     'date': e[2],                     'consumption_kwh': float(e[3])                 })                 total_kwh += float(e[3])             except:                 continue     energy_summary = {'total_kwh': total_kwh, 'estimated_cost': total_kwh * 0.12}     return render_template('energy_report.html', energy_summary=energy_summary, energy_logs=energy_logs, filter_date=filter_date)  # Route: activity log GET @app.route('/activity') def activity_logs():     search_text = request.args.get('search_text', '').strip().lower()     activities = []     activity_raw = read_pipe_file(ACTIVITY_LOGS_FILE, expected_fields=5)     devices_raw = read_pipe_file(DEVICES_FILE, expected_fields=13)      device_map = {}     for d in devices_raw:         try:             device_map[int(d[1])] = d[3]         except:             continue      for a in activity_raw:         try:             timestamp = a[1]             device_id = int(a[2])             action = a[3]             details = a[4]             device_name = device_map.get(device_id, '')             if search_text and search_text not in action.lower() and search_text not in details.lower():                 continue             activities.append({                 'timestamp': timestamp,                 'device_id': device_id,                 'device_name': device_name,                 'action': action,                 'details': details             })         except:             continue     return render_template('activity_logs.html', activities=activities, search_text=search_text)  # Route: activity search POST @app.route('/activity/search', methods=['POST']) def activity_search_post():     search_text = request.form.get('search_text', '').strip()     return redirect(url_for('activity_logs', search_text=search_text))  if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Endpoint                  | HTTP Method | Function Name          | Rendered Template               | Context Variables (Name: Type)                                                     |
|---------------------------|-------------|------------------------|--------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /** (root)                | GET         | root_redirect          | redirect to dashboard           | None                                                                              |
| /dashboard                | GET         | dashboard              | dashboard.html                 | devices_summary: dict (total: int, active: int, offline: int)
  rooms_summary: list of dict {room_name: str, device_count: int}            |
| /devices                  | GET         | device_list            | device_list.html               | devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, device_type: str, room: str, status: str}                      |
| /device/<int:device_id>   | GET         | device_control         | device_control.html            | device: dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, status: str, power: str, brightness: (int or None), temperature: (int or None), mode: str} |
| /device/<int:device_id>/control | POST        | device_control_post    | redirect to /device/<device_id> or error page | updated device data from form (handled internally)                             |
| /add_device               | GET         | add_device             | add_device.html                | rooms: list of str (room names)
  device_types: list of str (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance)                      |
| /add_device               | POST        | add_device_post        | redirect to /devices or error page | new device data from form (handled internally)                                |
| /automation               | GET         | automation_rules       | automation.html                | rules: list of dict {rule_id: int, rule_name: str, trigger_type: str, trigger_value: str, action_device_id: int, action_type: str, enabled: bool}
  devices: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str}                      |
| /automation               | POST        | add_automation_rule    | redirect to /automation or error page | new automation rule data from form (handled internally)                      |
| /energy                   | GET         | energy_report          | energy_report.html             | energy_summary: dict (total_kwh: float, estimated_cost: float)
  energy_logs: list of dict {device_id: int, device_name: str, date: str, consumption_kwh: float}
  filter_date: str or None                                                   |
| /energy/filter            | POST        | energy_filter_post     | redirect to /energy or error page | filter_date: str (parsed from form)                                          |
| /activity                 | GET         | activity_logs          | activity_logs.html             | activities: list of dict {timestamp: str, device_id: int, device_name: str, action: str, details: str}
  search_text: str or None                                                    |
| /activity/search          | POST        | activity_search_post   | redirect to /activity or error page | search_text: str (from form)                                                  |

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Smart Home Dashboard
- Element IDs:
  - dashboard-page: Div - Main container for dashboard page
  - device-summary: Div - Summary display (total devices, active, offline counts)
  - device-list-button: Button - Navigate to Device List (url_for('device_list'))
  - add-device-button: Button - Navigate to Add Device (url_for('add_device'))
  - automation-button: Button - Navigate to Automation Rules (url_for('automation_rules'))
  - energy-button: Button - Navigate to Energy Report (url_for('energy_report'))
  - activity-button: Button - Navigate to Activity Logs (url_for('activity_logs'))
  - room-list: Div - List of rooms with device counts

### 2. templates/device_list.html
- Page Title: My Devices
- Element IDs:
  - device-list-page: Div - Main container
  - device-table: Table - Showing all devices with columns name, type, room, status, actions
  - control-device-button-{device_id}: Button - Navigate to Device Control (url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))
  - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to Dashboard (url_for('dashboard'))

### 3. templates/add_device.html
- Page Title: Add New Device
- Element IDs:
